The Rolls-Royce Wraith is a luxury grand tourer introduced by Rolls-Royce in 2013. It is known for its combination of high performance, opulent features, and distinctive design. Here is a comprehensive overview of the Rolls-Royce Wraith: ### Design and Exterior - **Body Style**: The Wraith is a two-door coupe with a fastback design. - **Dimensions**: It measures about 207.9 inches in length, 76.7 inches in width, and 59.3 inches in height, with a wheelbase of 122.5 inches. - **Distinctive Features**: The Wraith features the iconic Rolls-Royce grille, coach doors (also known as suicide doors), and a sleek roofline that gives it a sporty yet elegant appearance. ### Engine and Performance - **Engine**: The Wraith is powered by a 6.6-liter twin-turbocharged V12 engine. - **Power Output**: It delivers around 624 horsepower and 605 lb-ft of torque. - **Transmission**: The engine is paired with an 8-speed automatic transmission. - **Performance**: The Wraith can accelerate from 0 to 60 mph in about 4.4 seconds, with a top speed electronically limited to 155 mph. ### Interior and Comfort - **Luxury Appointments**: The interior is handcrafted with the finest materials, including premium leather, wood veneers, and metal accents. - **Technology**: Features include a state-of-the-art infotainment system with a large central display, a bespoke audio system, and advanced navigation. - **Comfort**: The Wraith offers a spacious cabin with plush seating, a starlight headliner (fiber-optic lights embedded in the roof to resemble a starry night), and climate control. ### Driving Experience - **Ride Quality**: The Wraith is known for its smooth and quiet ride, thanks to its advanced suspension system and sound insulation. - **Handling**: Despite its size, the Wraith handles well, providing a comfortable yet engaging driving experience. ### Customization - **Bespoke Options**: Rolls-Royce offers extensive customization options, allowing buyers to personalize their Wraith with unique paint colors, interior trims, and bespoke features. - **Special Editions**: Over the years, there have been various special editions of the Wraith, featuring unique design elements and exclusive fin
